Sweet, strong and noble but waaaaay too self sacrificing.<br/>-St. Ryssa, no longer a saint<br/>-Epic battle between the Atlantian Gods <br/>-Styxx being a Chnotonian/God Killer<br/>-Urian!<br/>-Simi's interfering <br/>-Bethany rocks! <br/><br/><b>What I did</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10230583274081063571" style="display:none">Re-read in 2015. <br /><br />Still don't like the first 75% of this book and I stand by what I originally stated. I do have a little more appreciation for the second part. Styxx is a sweetie, but the book is still to black and white. <br /><br /><br /><b> review from 2013</b><br /><b>What I liked:</b> <br />-Styxx. He is a good character. Sweet, strong and noble but waaaaay too self sacrificing.<br />-St. Ryssa, no longer a saint<br />-Epic battle between the Atlantian Gods <br />-Styxx being a Chnotonian/God Killer<br />-Urian!<br />-Simi's interfering <br />-Bethany rocks! <br /><br /><b>What I didn't like: </b><br />- The 600+ pages of rape and (public) gang rapes, incest, child abuse, violence, humiliation and degradation. It was not in line with the other books, except Acheron's, but even that book did not contain the level of explicitness that Styxx's book had. Nor did it have the balance of that book. <br /><br />- Did an editor even see this book? Or did she have a carte blanche with her publisher for there to be that many explicit and semi-explicit scene's of incest, rape, (public) gang rapes of a 14 year old up until his majority? Seriously, while most of it was fade to black, there was enough of it to turn my stomach. (And this from someone who reads hardcore m/m BDSM)<br /><br />- There was a lot of switching perspectives and twisting characters around compared to previous stories. While I liked that for instance Ryssa was not the saint she was portrayed to be in the previous books, a lot of characters – including Acheron – became cardboard stereotypes of evil and wrong done to Styxx. His father was actually the most believable character. It was hard to grasp that every servant, every instructor, every senator or other person was against Styxx and only wanted to hurt him in some way. It was waaaaaaay to black and white. <br /><br />- The inconsistencies. We know Sherrilyn Kenyon has a tendency to twist the previous stories to suit her needs (which up until now has been mostly okay), but this book contains a lot of inconsistencies. There is Artemis and her scheming that doesn't add up that is then conveniently forgotten and forgiven (I would be pissed off if I was put on an island for over 11,000 years). Styxx's behavior and actions in past books and in particular Acheron's book that don't add up to this one. The nature of the Gods. How could Savitar not have known (there is a weak explanation in the book) or Ash. That he could have forgotten as a human, I could grasp, but not as a God.<br /><br />- What also bothered me (and that falls in line with the black and white characters) is the number of people in on the torture of Styxx and even Acheron. The number of senators and other people who went along with the rapes of Styxx and Estes schemes without his father actually knowing or the lack of rumors. There were some, but not too many. It didn't make sense. Didn't they realize he was a prince that would make their life miserable once he was on the throne? The unsupervised punishments were also a question mark. No prince would be punished without someone supervising to prevent exactly some of the scenes in the book. <br /><br />- Then there was the part where Styxx was on an Island (or two) for over 11,000 years. That is a bloody long time with no company and having to fend for yourself. There is a terrible concept of time in this book series, but to be alone for so long and still sane? Yeah. Not working for me much. And how could he still want to help those who put him there after all that has happened to him? And then there was Ash putting him back on an island which doesn't add up either except as a filler and show everyone that Ash is asshole. <br /><br />- There was no real romance to speak of. Only glimpses. <br /><br />Really, Styxx himself was a sweet character and I liked him a lot, but there was no balance in this story. The torture is drawn out for over 600+ pages before the actual story started and that was over way too quickly. There should have been an equal balance, but there wasn't. <br /><br />Up until now I have liked all of the Dark- Were- and Dream Hunter books out there. They always have been between 4 and 5 stars. This one is the first one that is truly not well done or thought out. I liked the idea of having Styxx's story, but this doesn't do him justice. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10230583274081063571" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_418392270" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/418392270" />
    <a title="Louise" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9627459-louise"><img alt="Louise" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1372421756p2/9627459.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/418392270?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Louise" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Louise" href="/user/show/9627459-louise">Louise</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17665263-styxx">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9627459-louise?shelf=love-it-read-it-begin-again">love-it-read-it-begin-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9627459-louise?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9627459-louise?shelf=dark-dream-and-were-hunters">dark-dream-and-were-hunters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9627459-louise?shelf=soul-shattering">soul-shattering</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer418392270" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14011192299715970989"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Be kind to everyone you meet, for we are all fighting a fierce battle.”<br/> -Plato<br/></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“...Life, like war, is neither right nor wrong. It just is. And rather than worry over a philosophy you can’t change, you should just try to live through it as best you can.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br/>Warning: the events in Styxx's life is very nauseating, do not attempt to read if you are not comfortable with raped, abuse, violence, w</span>
  <span id="freeText14011192299715970989" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Be kind to everyone you meet, for we are all fighting a fierce battle.”<br /> -Plato<br /></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“...Life, like war, is neither right nor wrong. It just is. And rather than worry over a philosophy you can’t change, you should just try to live through it as best you can.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br />Warning: the events in Styxx's life is very nauseating, do not attempt to read if you are not comfortable with raped, abuse, violence, war, degradation, and torture and other acts of inhumane proportions.<br />and read the book Acheron first before this.<br /><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>Time can heal a broken heart, but can anything save a shattered soul?</b>
</blockquote><br /><br />You think Acheron, Darling or even Zhadist from BDB got it worst in their life then you haven't met Styxx.<br /><br /><br />as the twin brother of Acheron, many had thought that Styxx was the arrogant, pampered prince who turned against Ash when he badly needed saving...not knowing that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ gods' pawns disguised themselves as Styxx in order to kidnapped the real Styxx so that the gods could raped him to no end <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />with the allure he has like his brother many people wanted him and physically abused his body. <br />His family hated him because they saw Acheron in his presence, his father had doubted he's one of them, his mother hated him for being born and even <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Ryssa, their sweet sister, while she was all caring to Ash, she had the worst to say towards Styxx <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />and as fuck up like his brother, he <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ feels the pain that Ash bore when he was tortured and degrade <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> a worst gift given to him by life.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>His brother wasn’t the only one damned. It was both of them. Two lives tied together in complete and utter misery.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Acheron thinks that just because he has it bad, I have it good.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />both brothers had it good when they where young, even abused by their father, they communicate like two little kids finding ways to be happy only for a little while...<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Will you keep it for me, Styxx? I would weep if it were lost.<i><br />Pulling it toward him, he cradled it to his chest. “I won’t let it be harmed, Acheron. It will be here for your return. I promise.”<br />No matter where they lived or how far apart, they were still brothers.<br />Forever and always.</i></i>
</blockquote><br /><br />until they were separated...<br />both their life has thrown into spiral, prejudice to both part got them in bitter hatred to each other because people around them feed them with false reality...<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Hatred was a lot easier to deal with than guilt or remorse. And memories that couldn’t be changed. Styxx knew that better than anyone.<br /><br />It’s amazing the damage we do to ourselves and others when all we’re trying to do is protect ourselves from being hurt. </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The truth is not always obvious, and it's never easy</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Styxx might be the best character so far, he exceeds Ash.<br />he was totally misunderstood by most people, I for one...I hate him in the book Acheron. I don't know his side of story until now and I never thought that I will love him way better than Ash.<br />He is humble, loyal and compassionate to those he loved even to Ash <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ if only Ash saw his true nature, but Ash was blinded by his grudges towards his brother <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />he wasn't the spoiled rotten prince people knew.<br />He cared to his men at war and he doesn't take anything for granted because he knows first hand how happiness can be stolen in just a glimpse.<br />there's only two people who loved and cared for him, and I loved them for taking good care of him.<br />What I love most about him was his strength and resilience, the pain he dealt with, the longings he'd gone through, he did give up most of the time, cos he wanted out of this life so badly. you will feel his emotion pouring out of the story. He endured it all. He survived. He's a better man through and through.<br />Another thing I like about him was his sarcasm, it's very sharp which made me laugh sometimes. His ability to hide his pain is what gets him into trouble because no one knows his true feelings.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>People make their own reality...A hundred people can witness the same exact event, and give two hundred and three different accountings of it.<br />“Everything is filtered through our emotions that change over time,...listen to both sides of every matter and try to find the truth that lies somewhere between the opposing accounts.”</i>
</blockquote><br />----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The most beautiful heart of all is the one that can still love even while it bleeds, and especially after its been broken into thousands of pieces.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />He never dared of finding love, when he jumped off a cliff to kill himself...<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[which eventually did not succeed cos he was bound to Ash's life force <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, he was founded by a beautiful blind woman who took care of him, she didn't know him and he gave him a false name because Styxx was scared that she might hate him too.<br />Her name was Bethany...<br />Bethany was the right hand of Dikastis, their god of justice. and in order not to judge others for what she saw, she is to be blind when she took human form. and also she's the Atlantean goddess of misery and wrath.<br />while Styxx was scared that Bethany might reject him for finding the truth that he was a the infamous prince most people falsely accused him to, Bethany was also afraid to tell him that she was a goddess.<br />not knowing that it wouldn't even matter because love have already bound their two hearts.<br /><br />Styxx and Bethany got the best love team ever and it spans through the years together and apart. unlike other couples who had it in a couple of weeks and declared their HEA.<br />they have the genuine love for each other and you can't help but support them against all odds for better or for worst...<br />Their love for each other was ordinary, a weary soldier and a simple girl which made it very special.<br />Their complete trust to each other and their vow of never letting go was the part that made me cry.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I will count the heartbeats until I see you again.”<br />“And I will make your count as brief as possible. I promise.”<br />...<br />“And I will be counting down every beat of my heart until we’re together.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />the very strong message of it is that Love is the source of strength from someone we dearly love and makes things alright even in the depths of darkness, the pulse that we hear for us to continue living and the light that will lead us back to their warm embrace...<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> ΔIΚΟΣ ΣΑΣ. <br />Faithfully yours.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Never once in my life did I feel sunshine on my skin until the day you touched me,” he breathed in her ear. “And without my Bethany, I dwell in total darkness.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>What they have was truly Heart felt, heart wrenching, beautifully tragic but also there's a Hope that it will find a way no matter what, a love so profound that even through the test of time, no matter how life will separate them, a <br /><i>HALF HEART WILL ALWAYS ALWAYS FINDS HIS OTHER HALF TO MAKE IT WHOLE AGAIN.</i></b><br />----------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br />There's a lot of going on in this book, a lot of twist and surprising revelations and I hope I have a dark hunter guide book to help me with all the characters, the enemies are still the enemies and and the good one's? well I love them and there's nothing to say.<br />one of my favorite heroes, Urian has an important role in this book.<br />I'm a little bit angry to Ash because he's the one who's holding grudges to Styxx. but I still love the man of course I love him, he's inspirational...just don't tell him that I have a soft spot towards Styxx lol:D<br />I thought I would never get a happy ending, the suffering that Styxx went through I thought it would not end happily but I'm glad it did.<br />I wanted to say more but my ramblings doesn't do any justice on how much I love this book. Every time I try and come here and made some editing work, a tear will fall, its just to much to bear, I don't even want to share this review. That's how tough it is. I will hold this book so dearly.<br /><br />Another amazing and torturous book from the master of fucked up PNR heroes Sherrilyn Kenyon. This is the best she got!<br /> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Styxx held his hand out to his brother. Acheron took it and allowed him to pull him to his feet.<br />They stared at each other, fully united for the first time since the day Estes had taken Acheron to Atlantis. Brothers forever and always.<br />Acheron hugged him close</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14011192299715970989" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1969887806" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1969887806?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=dark-or-taboo">dark-or-taboo</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=hybrid-multiple-genre">hybrid-multiple-genre</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=general-fantasy-and-mythology">general-fantasy-and-mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=made-me-emotional">made-me-emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=favorite-book-guys">favorite-book-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1969887806" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4303184213604863459"><b>You are one twisted woman, Sherrilyn Kenyon.</b> How could you make me love this impossibly disturbing book? <i>How???</i><br/><br/>*Trigger warning : extreme rape, abuse and gore* from what I can remember. I'm reviewing this book months after I read it. <br/><br/><b>4.5 stars</b> I hesitated for a minute over the thought of adding <i>Styxx</i> to my favorites shelf since favorites tend to equal recommendations, yet I've struggled so much with this series that I find it hard to recommend. There are so many weak books in Dark Hunter lineup </span>
  <span id="freeText4303184213604863459" style="display:none"><b>You are one twisted woman, Sherrilyn Kenyon.</b> How could you make me love this impossibly disturbing book? <i>How???</i><br><br>*Trigger warning : extreme rape, abuse and gore* from what I can remember. I'm reviewing this book months after I read it. <br><br><b>4.5 stars</b> I hesitated for a minute over the thought of adding <i>Styxx</i> to my favorites shelf since favorites tend to equal recommendations, yet I've struggled so much with this series that I find it hard to recommend. There are so many weak books in Dark Hunter lineup that it honestly surprises me when an <i>incredible</i> book comes along from out of nowhere and blows my mind like this one did. However, <i>Styxx</i> is now a favorite book, and so to the shelf it goes. <br><br>But let's get to the star of this story. <i>***Very slight character spoilers ahead. No major plot spoilers.***</i> I will mention Styxx's abuse with the assumption that most people will know that his abuse was going to happen in his book. He is after all the twin of a man who was severely abused, and this story is the other side of the coin<br><br><b>Once Upon a Time</b> I hated Styxx. True story. <br><br>I had something to say about him on my review for his brother Acheron's book. I was positive that Styxx would not find redemption. I pretty much deemed it impossible. <br><br><i>Yes, I will take that plate of crow now.</i> Maybe Simi will let me borrow her BBQ sauce.<br><br>I don't have much in the way of pretty words to describe a book that rips your heart out. Before Styxx came along in the series, my favorite book was Ash's. Before Styxx came along, my favorite character was Ash. Dare I say that Styxx might have edged Ash out? <br><br>Wait, no. Ash is still my favorite character. But Styxx won the book race. <br><br>In some ways, I was less emotional when reading Styxx's story. So much of his story was a different spin on what happened to Ash, so I was slightly desensitized to the extreme abuse having gone through it before (only slightly though. There were definitely some scenes that hit me right in the feels).<br><br>In some ways, I was more emotional. Kenyon took a character that I'd hated and made me love him - from <i>out of nowhere</i>. Then, all of a sudden, I was invested. And I wasn't ready. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471312845ra/20025585.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Through all of this, I didn't lose any respect for Ash like some other fans did. Ash went through hell, and on top of all of that he'd sacrificed for others for thousands of years without asking for anything in return. People have treated him like a servant for as long as he's been alive, even his precious Dark Hunters. He deserved to have each and every last little shit fit that he wanted to throw, and had every right to be bitter and mistrusting of anyone and everyone, <i>especially</i> Styxx. Period. <br><br>But wow, I might have felt more sorry for Styxx. I didn't think that was <i>ever</i> possible. I wanted to cuddle him so much. I might have even had a moment or two when his sexiness surpassed Ash's for me. Again, HOW???<br><br>Well played, Kenyon. You managed to pull out the stops. This book messed with me well and good. If you could write like this every time, you would be on my favorites shelf a whole hell of a lot.<br><br>If I had to mention a negative, I think the shock factor became played out after a while. After the first couple of dozen intense scenes, I started to become detached again because it got repetitive. <br><br>Okay, wait, there's a second negative. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[This scene : <i>"Really, Styxx, it's nothing to be ashamed of. Estes has always had a preference for men, and it's never bothered me."<br><br>Styxx sat in stunned silence as hatred flowed thick through his veins. (he thought) You knew how he was and you turned me loose with him?</i><br><br>Styxx was molested by his uncle. His father acknowledged that his uncle was gay, yet let Styxx's uncle take him in to live with him.<br><br><b>Being gay is not equal to, nor does it make you a molester.</b> I doubt that Kenyon meant to imply this, but that's how the scene read, and it bothers me that those two things would be tied together. There are plenty of straight people who molest family members. Being gay is not the catalyst to that kind of sickness. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="4303184213604863459" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1481976176" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1481976176" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1481976176?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Dark Hunter fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=greek-mythology">greek-mythology</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1481976176" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13913016184940159166"><b>
  <i>"I love you, Acheron."<br/>"I love you too, brother."<br/>"Do you think we'll ever be able to leave this place and find peace?"<br/>"No. I think we were born to suffer."<br/>"At least we have each other."<br/>Acheron nodded. "Brothers - always and forever."</i>
</b><br/><br/>If you were ever a fan of this series, and she lost you at some point between Acheron and this book, let me encourage you to read this one. It completely changes everything you thought you knew about Ash's past. In other words:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451340959i/17529219.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book is a lot like Acheron. The </span>
  <span id="freeText13913016184940159166" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"I love you, Acheron."<br>"I love you too, brother."<br>"Do you think we'll ever be able to leave this place and find peace?"<br>"No. I think we were born to suffer."<br>"At least we have each other."<br>Acheron nodded. "Brothers - always and forever."</i>
</b><br><br>If you were ever a fan of this series, and she lost you at some point between Acheron and this book, let me encourage you to read this one. It completely changes everything you thought you knew about Ash's past. In other words:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451340959i/17529219.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is a lot like Acheron. The first part is the past and the second part is present time. The past goes through the same events in Ash's life, from Styxx's point of view. If you think you knew Styxx, you are thoroughly mistaken. We all knew his dad was a horrible dick, so why did we assume that he didn't question Styxx's paternity too?<br><br><b>
  <i>"you look like us, but are you really my son?"<br>"You look so human... but are you human? I have to know." Before Styxx could move or react, his father seized his forearm in a merciless grip then he violently slashed it open.</i>
</b><br><br>Also, we all saw the way Ryssa hated Styxx in Ash's book, but we never saw WHY she hated him when he was just a young boy. Was it his fault that Ash's parents were jerks? Why couldn't Ryssa love both brothers? Did she have a one-brother allotment for her love?<br><br><i>
  <b>She glared at him as if it was his fault that Acheron was gone. "What do you want, you selfish little beast?"<br>"I could be your little brother too. Like Acheron."<br>"You? You're the reason they took my brother from me. Just because you look like him doesn't make you what he is. You're just a poor copy of him. Get out of my sight. You sicken me."</b>
</i><br><br>So, this book changes everything, and in a good way. Contrary to what some other readers felt, I didn't like Ash less after reading it. He was a victim of his past and his perception was skewed by his circumstances and Ryssa's vitriol. Plus, he does finally figure things out.<br><br>But, there is a lot of frustration when reading this story because it is one of those things where a 30 minute conversation could have prevented thousands of years of suffering. I guess men would rather suffer in silence than actually talk about their feelings. Am I right, girls? ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451340959i/17529220.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Men: Not known for their communications skills.<br><br>So many things are revealed, and change, in this book. I love Urian, who was Stryker's son that is now Ash's ally. He is awesome in this story and I can't wait for him to have his own book.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13913016184940159166" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_603934500" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/603934500" />
    <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth"><img alt="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487525094p2/13870608.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/603934500?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth">Jo ★The Book Sloth★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=insta-love-lust">insta-love-lust</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=kick-ass-heroine">kick-ass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=gods-come-out-to-play">gods-come-out-to-play</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer603934500" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16088850795309541726">I think I'll give this one a 4. Maybe a 4,5 or a 4,75. Oh, screw it. It's a 5!!!<br/><br/>Where to begin with this one? You think you know your characters and then "BOOM", the skies open, the fires roar and suddenly you're in a new world. Let me explain...<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Styxx</u>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419659i/832307.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>See that gorgeous guy? That's Ash's twin the infamous Styxx. Before his book Styxx was an arrogant guy who saw the light to me. Boy was I wrong Styxx's life was an even bigger tragedy than Acheron's. Everything bad that happened to Ash happened </span>
  <span id="freeText16088850795309541726" style="display:none">I think I'll give this one a 4. Maybe a 4,5 or a 4,75. Oh, screw it. It's a 5!!!<br><br>Where to begin with this one? You think you know your characters and then "BOOM", the skies open, the fires roar and suddenly you're in a new world. Let me explain...<br><br><b>
  <u>Styxx</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419659i/832307.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>See that gorgeous guy? That's Ash's twin the infamous Styxx. Before his book Styxx was an arrogant guy who saw the light to me. Boy was I wrong Styxx's life was an even bigger tragedy than Acheron's. Everything bad that happened to Ash happened to Styxx as well. And were Ash had at least one or two people who loved him uncoditionally Styxx had no one. He grew up in a violent family, with negligent and many times cruel parents, two siblings who begrudged him every breath, an asshole for an uncle. He was just so caring and loving that you couldn't help siding with him every single time. The one light in his life was Beth and she was taken from him as well. I think I cried the whole way through the book.<br><br><b>
  <u>Beth</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419659i/832308._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved Beth. She was a nice girl(goddess), fresh and hopefull but she wasn't a naive little virgin. She knew what she wanted and did what she had to get it. She wasn't unnecesarily cruel but she was no pushover either. I enjoyed her snarky side. I think that generally she was one of SK's best heroines so far.<br><br><b>
  <u>Acheron</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400429i/775938.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am so used to rooting for Ash that I was so majorly disappointed by the fact that he behaved like a jerk. Styxx tried so freakin hard and every time he got only a slap in return. If Ash was a real life person I'd have slapped some sense into him but I won't get the satisfaction. *sad face*<br><br><b>
  <u>Ryssa</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419659i/832309.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What a selfish bitch. I didn't have much love for her in Acheron's book and I actually hate her in this one. Ash had some excuses for his behaviour but this jealous, spoiled brat had none at all. Every time someone said something good for Styxx or did sth good for him(usually by accident) she was there to poison the moment. She was the only one being spoiled and loved by everyone and she begrudged Styxx every moment of success.<br><br><b>
  <u>Apollo</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379795037i/600067.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now Apollo makes Artemis look like a harmless little kitten. The things this guy does. He is just so perverted and cruel that I don't have the words to describe him. I won't try. Just be prepared for hard-core abuse.<br><br>I can go on and on and on. There are so many characters in this book that I won't be able to sum it up if I continue. What you have to be prepared for...<br><br>1) Two revelations concerning characters we love. *faint*<br>2) The "baddie" for me(which you won't get if you haven't read my reviews so bad for you).<br>3) Prepare to change your mind for many people.<br>4) Much blabbering.<br>5) Gods from both Greek and Egyptian pantheons. *fangirling*<br><br>Okay...Here I must add some things because it's very obvious were I got bored with writing this. It will be even more spoilerish than the previous so stand warned.<br><br>I loved the book. I loved it but still some things annoyed me. To begin with it had the same problem as Acheron's. The "past" part was too long. Yes it didn't exactly drag but it was too emotionally loaded and got a tiny bit tiring by the time you finished it. It was important that we knew these things to be able to invest on Styxx's happiness but it could have been described with less words. Thank god for Galen or I would have dropped the book just because I couldn't bare the bleakness.<br><br>Then came the "modern" part which wasn't bad but it wasn't good either. I mean the dessert? Really? How....Boring. It was so uninteresting. All the other heroes had violence and risks and excitement in their live. Styxx decided to live in a tent with the sand for company. It was a bit dissapointing tbh.<br><br>And of course in the end everything had to resolve in about 10 seconds flat. The only positive was the Urian thing. I loved that little surprise there.<br><br>PS. Did you see the next book's blurb? Why two strangers? I want Savitar(with Apollymi or I'll be really disappointed) or Urian damn it! I want them yesterday.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16088850795309541726" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/711729900?book_show_action=true">Sep 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ms. Nikki" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ms. Nikki" href="/user/show/3291712-ms-nikki">Ms. Nikki</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3291712-ms-nikki?shelf=own-it-pb-or-hc">own-it-pb-or-hc</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer711729900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3598417800633638556">*******************BIG ASS SPOILERS AHEAD*****************************<br/><br/>Ahem *clears throat from all the bullshit I just swallowed* It leaves a bitter aftertaste. <br/><br/>First, so I won't be a complete bi-atch. It's totally awesome that authors take the time to write, sometimes to the exclusion of family and a life. Not to mention carpal tunnel and hemorrhoids. I have not been able to make myself finish my own writing, so I know it takes determination, will-power, time, and self-motivation.<br/><br/>I have really </span>
  <span id="freeText3598417800633638556" style="display:none">*******************BIG ASS SPOILERS AHEAD*****************************<br /><br />Ahem *clears throat from all the bullshit I just swallowed* It leaves a bitter aftertaste. <br /><br />First, so I won't be a complete bi-atch. It's totally awesome that authors take the time to write, sometimes to the exclusion of family and a life. Not to mention carpal tunnel and hemorrhoids. I have not been able to make myself finish my own writing, so I know it takes determination, will-power, time, and self-motivation.<br /><br />I have really enjoyed Kenyon's Dark-Hunter series and Acheron put the icing on the cake. I feared that she could not out-do herself and to my utter disappointed she didn't. <br /><br />If you're Kenyon's butt buddy and are not mature enough to understand everyone has their own opinion, look away now, for I do not intentionally set out to hurt feelings..<br /><br />This book was: <br /><br />Frivolous: unworthy of serious or sensible treatment<br /><br />incongruous: out of keeping or place; inappropriate; unbecoming<br /><br />inconsistent:lacking agreement, as one thing with another or two or more things in relation to each other<br /><br />filler:an object or substance used to add weight or size to something or to fill in a gap <br /><br />600 Pages of Suffering:<br /><br />1. Styxx took the beatings in stride, always protecting his brother.<br />2. Everyone (emphasis on everyone) hated, no, loathed Styxx with a passion. We're talking about a little boy, since the moment he was born.<br />3. The hating and abuse never really let up.<br />4. His mother drinks herself into a stupor wishing she'd never birthed her or Acheron and says so constantly.<br />5. The mother slaps him.<br />6. The mother stabs him 20 some times.<br />7. His sister Ryssa constantly wishes he would die and be raped.<br />8. Acheron is raped and beaten.<br />9. Styxx is raped and owned.<br />10. Acheron is taken away by his incestuous uncle Estes, who whores him out to everyone who actually wants a piece of Styxx, since they are twins.<br />11. Acheron is drugged and turned away from his brother.<br />12. Styxx tries to help him escape, but this new bitch-ass Acheron tells on him and Styxx gets branded physically and raped for like 2 months while Acheron laughs.<br />13. Ryssa hates him some more and slaps him at least 20 times in this book. I wish I had the ebook to look up how many times it was typed. If you include Xerses, Estes, Ryssa, and his mom, I'm sure it's over 50 times at different time periods in the book. THAT GOT ON MY NERVES SO BAD.<br />14.Okay, I felt sorrow for Styxx after his first, second, and fifth smackdown, but by the 15th he's starting to look like a wimpy punk.<br />15. Galen beat the snot out of him for years, but magically on the 1,110 training session, he feels he went too far and starts to respect him and not look at him as a stuck-up brat, then call him SON. What the HEE-HAW?!?!?!?!?!?!<br />15. Styxx is a bad mamma-jamma when he's on the battlefield kicking god-children and giants asses, but come home and Appolo throws him across the room like a football and Xerses punches him in the ribs and kick him?<br />16. Ryssa smacks him some more and scratches him with her nails.<br />17. Acheron, Ryssa, and their mom try to kill him.<br />18. Styxx was constantly put between a rock and a hard place and no one. I mean NO ONE was there for him until he met Bethany. (oh, and Galen)<br />19. What? Artemis lied about Styxx. *sarcastic voice* She would never do that.<br />20. Characters were flipping the script left and right, doing things totally out of character. Galen was the biggest and then when Xerses started loving on him, then when Acheron said "brothers" near the end of the book like they were about to tag into a ring to fight.<br />21. What about the bullshit way everything was told to Acheron at the end of the book to get him to feel for Styxx? Sav said he wasn't going to tell him anything saying something like, "some thinga are best not known or remembered." Then he goes on to tell him all the things that happened to Styxx and how Acheron knew about it. <br />22. Oh, and the end. I just couldn't kill your baby. Turn around, he's right there.<br /><br /><br />My main peeve is all the rape. We get it! He was horribly abused and he's still a good guy even though he went through so much. I didn't count, but he was getting raped or beaten for like 600 pages. The boy got raped right before he went to go see his girlfriend. <br /><br /><br />ARE YOU KIDDING ME????????????? THIS IS CONSIDERED GOOD FICTION????????<br /><br /><br />I wanted Styxx to die so I didn't have to read anymore of this book. I hate that I read how wimpy Styxx was and how Acheron was a complete asshole. I now see him in a different light. Styxx to me, was no hero. They didn't even let him have that glory. The best part of this book was when he was fighting and that ended all too soon. I didn't even care that Bethany was back by the end of the book. This book sucked the happiness out of me. No Joke.<br /><br />If this was a first time author it would have gotten more hell over the constant raping. Even though it is not described in excessive detail, it came up way too much to not have your mind go there. There was no skimming it. There was no pretending it wasn't happening. This whole book was overdone and I'm finished chewing on it. I'd rather a great book with fantastic characters be 300 pages than 600 pages of repetition and filler.<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_711566348" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/711566348" />
    <a title="Lil" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/954295-lil"><img alt="Lil" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1209586411p2/954295.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/711566348?book_show_action=true">Sep 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lil" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lil" href="/user/show/954295-lil">Lil</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/954295-lil?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer711566348" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4235568637495929586"><br/><br/>From the first time we met him, I, like so many other fans of Sherrilyn Kenyon's Dark Hunter series, hated Styxx. He was our hero's twin. The evil one. The one who hated his brother Acheron, and wished him no good, ever.<br/><br/>Sherrilyn Kenyon blows all that to hell with Styxx's story.<br/><br/>And I'm so glad she did.<br/><br/>Styxx, the hero of Didymos, the future King of the two islands that make up the Greek City-State. He's the Heir. And you would think that he has it easy. Only, that's not true. He has it as hard, o</span>
  <span id="freeText4235568637495929586" style="display:none"><br /><br />From the first time we met him, I, like so many other fans of Sherrilyn Kenyon's Dark Hunter series, hated Styxx. He was our hero's twin. The evil one. The one who hated his brother Acheron, and wished him no good, ever.<br /><br />Sherrilyn Kenyon blows all that to hell with Styxx's story.<br /><br />And I'm so glad she did.<br /><br />Styxx, the hero of Didymos, the future King of the two islands that make up the Greek City-State. He's the Heir. And you would think that he has it easy. Only, that's not true. He has it as hard, or harder than his brother Acheron has ever had it. But he can't show it. So, he shores up his defenses, becomes the best warrior and cuts a huge swath through the Atlanteans while they're at war, gaining the total respect of his warriors.<br /><br />But once they're called home, his family is still the same. His father hates him, his mother and sister do too, and his brother is still gone. Taken when they were only seven.<br /><br />After all the horror of his childhood, Styxx finds a woman whom he loves dearly, and though she protests at first, and holds her own secrets from him, eventually consents to marry him. What should be the happiest days of his life turn to ashes in his mouth and Styxx is again left with nothing.<br /><br />Where he goes from there, and none of what happens to him, is the easiest story to read. It hurts and I cried through a lot of it. But I also laughed and the end? Was absolutely worth what he went through.<br /><br />There are some big secrets about the Dark-Hunter world that come to light in this one, and we find out that our hero from previous books, Acheron, is sometimes all-too-human in his emotions.That even he, can allow pain and bad memories or what other people think, cloud his judgement.<br /><br />Nothing is ever just black and white. Nothing.<br /><br />Read Styxx. If you're a Dark-Hunter fan, it's a must. In my opinion, best book in the series since Acheron.<br /><br />Thank you, Sherri. For listening to Styxx tell you his story, even though at first, you didn't want to.<br /></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_711551444" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/711551444" />
    <a title="Delilah Stephans" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1121381-delilah-stephans"><img alt="Delilah Stephans" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1241111966p2/1121381.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/711551444?book_show_action=true">Sep 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Delilah Stephans" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Delilah Stephans" href="/user/show/1121381-delilah-stephans">Delilah Stephans</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer711551444" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10776867068884645472">Okay, I'll admit it - I came into this book with very low expectations. Honestly my thought was "Oh she's going to reform Styxx and turn him into a hero - whatever." <br/><br/>The review part of the book - where Acheron and Styxx's books overlapped realy didn't effect me. But the things that weren't in Acheron - yeah those got to me. But what had me tearing up was when Acheron finally realized what a bastard he'd been. Now I love Ash and his story broke my heart - to this day I haven't read the first half</span>
  <span id="freeText10776867068884645472" style="display:none">Okay, I'll admit it - I came into this book with very low expectations. Honestly my thought was "Oh she's going to reform Styxx and turn him into a hero - whatever." <br /><br />The review part of the book - where Acheron and Styxx's books overlapped realy didn't effect me. But the things that weren't in Acheron - yeah those got to me. But what had me tearing up was when Acheron finally realized what a bastard he'd been. Now I love Ash and his story broke my heart - to this day I haven't read the first half of his book again - but he was every bit as self absorbed as Styxx was accused of being.<br /><br />Ryssa - okay hate away for this but I never really bought the goody-goody long-suffering put upon view Ash had of her. No one is that GOOD and never loses their temper or gets snotty - please. Styxx's book - well I don't fully believe that version of her either - I think there is truth in both books.<br /><br />I loved Bethany! And whoo boy! The twist about Urian at the end? I was smiling and pumping my fist YES!<br /><br />I'm editing this after reading some other reviews - was the book graphic? Yes. That never really upset me. Mainly because it made such complete sense of things in previous books. Yes I was one of those that thought when Ash poofed his brother off in an earlier book that it was harsh and unfeeling. I didn't like Ash for that, understood it but didn't like it. Now I am so much angrier at Ash for it.</span>

  <span id="freeText5859552565169790491" style="display:none">Wait a minute...Styxx? What the heck? What happened to Jaden's book? What about Savitar? I say stop introducing characters and forgetting that you left their story open, and wait years to address again...it is very annoying (end of rant!).<br /><br />8/7 - I per-ordered this in Audio (31 hours!!!!!)...I will be writing a review as soon as I am done (There had better be some Savitar and Jaden in this...I will take some Vane at this point...) I have been skipping thru most of this book...<br /><br />9/4 - All done! What a ride. Great job, Ms. Kenyon. Loved the ending (great twist!) Hope to see these two more in the future...</span>

<div id="review_735160439" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/735160439" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/735160439?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781405528214" href="/book/show/18386252-styxx">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=october-reads">october-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer735160439" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1878066202831478379"><br/>"The most beautiful heart of all <br/>is the one that can still love even while it bleeds,<br/>and especially after it's been shattered into thousands of pieces."<br/><br/>First I want to say thank you to my Buddies who experienced this book with, or listened to me whine about how upset I was during the reading of this book! Thank you to Steph, BK, and Paula; I truly appreciated your support while going on this emtional journey.<br/><br/>Wow! I can't believe that I made it through over 900 pages; which I will add that most o</span>
  <span id="freeText1878066202831478379" style="display:none"><br />"The most beautiful heart of all <br />is the one that can still love even while it bleeds,<br />and especially after it's been shattered into thousands of pieces."<br /><br />First I want to say thank you to my Buddies who experienced this book with, or listened to me whine about how upset I was during the reading of this book! Thank you to Steph, BK, and Paula; I truly appreciated your support while going on this emtional journey.<br /><br />Wow! I can't believe that I made it through over 900 pages; which I will add that most of them were heartbreaking and at times so gruesome I felt physically ill. Sherrilyn Kenyon is the one author that has always been able to pull me into her world that she has created, as if I were living there myself. I also feel like I am experiencing the characters life through their eyes and body, and it usually leaves me quite drained once I am finished. In the case of "Styxx," it was one of the hardest books I have ever read, and I am literally feeling as if I have been on a ride through the house of terrors. My biggest complaint for his book is that out of 900 plus pages, about 100 of them were about something happy. That means 100 pages not together, but sporadically placed through out the book. That was just not enough! This man was put through hell and then some. There was so much torture, rape, and humiliation that it felt like that was the main theme of the book. I see no reason why there was so much. It felt like SK was trying to make Styxx's life 50 times worse than Acheron's; which was terrible enough. I think she could have got her point across that Styxx was absolutely tormented and reviled without dragging it on for most of the book. This was the reason I rated it four stars instead of five. <br />This book was done in two parts, just as Acheron's was. The difference between the two is that by the second part in Acheron's, we got a love story and a reprieve from all of the horrendous torture and pain he had to endure. With Styxx's, the second part of the book didn't end his misery. Yes, there was torture and rape, but there was mostly lonliness, sadness, and terrible luck. My heart bled for that guy, to the point that I just wanted to scream, "Enough already...I get it..his life sucks!!!"<br /><br />As for the good, I fell in love with Styxx; which is something I honestly didn't think SK would be able to get me to do. He was truly a hero in my eyes, and his love for Bethany was one of the deepest loves I have ever read about. To love her and stay faithful to her for over 11 thousand years...amazing! Better yet, she loved him with the same loyalty, and when she fought for him, I was cheering her on out loud!! (I really did get into this book!!) Even though, we didn't get near enough time with Bethany and Styxx; there will never be a romance that could ever top these two in my eyes. It was EPIC!! I just wish I had more of them; but maybe that contributed to the beauty, not having enough made me crave them even more!<br /><br />Acheron was picked apart by the readers, and I can understand why as he came across as a heartless prick most of the time. I don't blame either Styxx or Acheron for their anger or their behaviour though. Both of them had been through hell and back, and they both had misconceptions and misinterpretations. They were a product of their environment. There were a few quotes that really stood out for me regarding the volatile relationship between the brothers:<br /><br />"It's amazing the damage we do to ourselves and others when all we're trying to do is protect ourselves from being hurt."<br /><br />"Every man, woman,and child is capable of extreme and utter prejudice and cruelty when they feel justified in their hatred....As Plato said, be kind to everyone you meet for we are all fighting difficult battles."<br /><br />"Our lives are marked and shaped by our regrets. THings we all want to take back but we can't. In a perfect world, we would never hurt the ones we love or cause hurt to befall them. But the world isn't perfect and neither are we."<br /><br />Such terrible things were done to both of them, and they lashed out due to their assumptions that each brother was the cause of some of their pain and suffering. There was also envy on both sides, each of them thinking the other was better off and wouldn't understand what they were going through. In reality, how could either one of them give any other human being trust, considering every single person in their lives had let them down in some way or another. The tortures and rapes were a part of the abuse; but their was also the constant ridicule and lack of love that fed their lives on a daily basis. I was glad to see Styxx and Acheron's relationship evolve, and I hope that they will keep healing their relationship in future books to come.<br />Ryssa, Acheron and Styxx's sister was a surprise in this book. She was a bitch, and I didn't like her at all. It was strange as she was so different in this book as she was in Acheron's. She gave all of her love to Ash, and all of her venom to Styxx. She came across as a spoiled brat and just plain mean. Again though, we see her in Styxx's perspective; who knows what she had endured through out her young life. <br /><br />It was wonderful to have a reunion with some of my favorite characters from past Dark-Hunter books! I love Simi, and especially some of her interactions with Styxx. It was sweet what she did for his birthday, and I loved how she called him "Akri-copy!" This scene added a much needed reprieve from all of the sadness.<br />This book has set us up for some more Dark Hunter books, and I can't wait to see who is up next. One thing about SK is she knows how to write and she does it extremely well. I am impressed that even though the series has twenty plus books; it's still going strong in my eyes. I admit the last few books weren't as great as others; but again, this has blew the series wide open again in my opinion. There is a lot more to come, and I am eager to see what is in store for Nick! I will remain a dedicated fan, and if you haven't given this series a try; but are wondering if you should or not? Do it! Very few series can beat this one, it has everything from humor,sex,violence, friendship, and sadness. It is series that has no equal, and characters that you will grow to love like friends and family.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1878066202831478379" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15848011194925501933">Thank the gods I lived through this. Beaten bruised, bloodied, and heartbroken, but I lived. Styxx, man I just keep shaking my head at his 11,000 years + of extreme torture. It didn't rip and gut me like Acheron's book did but it hurt. Acheron's book took me out of this series for two years. Recovery time for this one, a couple days. What ? am I just so jaded now I can take it easier ? Isn't that a dark thought. I think Ms. Kenyon did everything imaginable she could think up to hurt and humiliat</span>
  <span id="freeText15848011194925501933" style="display:none">Thank the gods I lived through this. Beaten bruised, bloodied, and heartbroken, but I lived. Styxx, man I just keep shaking my head at his 11,000 years + of extreme torture. It didn't rip and gut me like Acheron's book did but it hurt. Acheron's book took me out of this series for two years. Recovery time for this one, a couple days. What ? am I just so jaded now I can take it easier ? Isn't that a dark thought. I think Ms. Kenyon did everything imaginable she could think up to hurt and humiliate him. Oh dang it lasted, and lasted and lasted and then it came back and slapped him upside his heart again ! It was too much for this reader, I was so grateful, relieved and exhausted when it ended. "Thank the gods it ended" Styxx finally got a life worth living, forgiveness was fast and to me unbelievable. I would have never forgiven 11 minutes of what he lived through and he did it fro 11,000+.<br />I am amazed at the details and massive amounts information juggled and placed just so, and it all worked. This author is truly amazing and cruel to her characters. : ) I'm on to the next one in line.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1479653315223955593"><b>*****Five and more definite eternally "forever and always" tear jerking sparkling stars!*****</b><br/><br/><i>This review came with warning, there's too much abuse, rape, explicit torturing sex scene,and so many tears will fall. Eternally torturing hero, prick little brother and siter's torturing, everybody torturing a hero, like it's not going to end! If you're a soft at heart, this one is NOT for you. Kenyon is a true soul slayer.</i><br/><br/><br/><b>Styxx and Acheron , the twins.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388931i/749816.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388931i/749817.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Honestly, this book turned my world upside down.   <span id="freeText1479653315223955593" style="display:none"><b>*****Five and more definite eternally "forever and always" tear jerking sparkling stars!*****</b><br><br><i>This review came with warning, there's too much abuse, rape, explicit torturing sex scene,and so many tears will fall. Eternally torturing hero, prick little brother and siter's torturing, everybody torturing a hero, like it's not going to end! If you're a soft at heart, this one is NOT for you. Kenyon is a true soul slayer.</i><br><br><br><b>Styxx and Acheron , the twins.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388931i/749816.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388931i/749817.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly, this book turned my world upside down. I used to believe that Ryssa was an angel, and Acheron was a damaged soul his twin caused. But Ryssa was a complete bitch here, I hate it how she threatened Styxx like that. But the fact was, Ash and Styxx, they’re both cursed, damaged.<br><br><b>This is Styxx POV.</b><br><br>I can read what’s on his mind now. <br>Styxx was LONELY. <br>Ash got Ryssa and the gods protection. But Styxx, he’s on his own. Alone. <br><br>And if you think, Acheron’s pain was hell, Styxx's doubled it. It was double hell for him. And I wanted to yell at Sherri why did she’s so cruel of making Styxx like this. Live wearing a mask as a spoiled Prince of Didymos, Styxx actually the most damaged, tortured soul. In his case, body and soul.<br><br>And don’t think even Hell won’t be like that. He destroyed, slayed into pieces. And I cried and cried and cried for him. How can I not? He keep it alone, all the rapes he had, all the torturing, all the hates he accepted from everyone…He’s sacrificed too much for whom? <b>Nobody deserved his untold sacrifice. Nobody.</b><br><br>I read Acheron a year ago,read about his painful, torturing youth,Styxx painful faith, covered what was I read in Acheron.<br>And shit! The incest was unbearable! <br><br>I really wanted to slap Ash and Ryssa in so many times...how can they're NOT see his pain, his loneliness?<br>While Ash and Ryssa laughing playing, he's been tortured and sick, and lonely...rejected from his own "family"&gt;<br>Family my ass!<br>His only family was JUST Galen!!!!<br><br>	<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Will you keep it for me, Styxx? I would weep if it were lost.Pulling it toward him, he cradled it to his chest. “I won’t let it be harmed, Acheron. It will be here for your return. I promise.”No matter where they lived or how far apart, they were still brothers.Forever and always." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br> And this one was part of his suffered tortured life...Apollo....!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379801022i/678412._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388931i/749818._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Until 90% how can't Ash was so prick??? And God! I really wanted to punch his face and ripped his hair and tear it and thrown him to the wall! Damn Ash!<br><b>Can't you "see",? Dammit!!!!</b><br>I cried a river while read what Savitar told Ash about Styxx, and what was Tory tried to made Ash see what he can't see all this time...<br><br>Thank God Styxx at least have Urian and Savitar while Ash acted like a total jerk!<br>And Urian him self <b>surprised</b> me for what he is...really surprised me...<br><br>What I loved about Styxx was, damn...this guy was a total faithful man...Bethany was so lucky having him!<br><br>I can see why Ash's fan base was so upset with this book, Ash here was...OMG! Am speechless....while Styxx is now my new hero...<br>Well...I never expected one bit I will like Styxx...but like I said earlier, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4430.Sherrilyn_Kenyon" title="Sherrilyn Kenyon" rel="nofollow noopener">Sherrilyn Kenyon</a> turned my world upside down like the sinked Atlantis...you can feel it while reading it.<br><br>"The most beautiful heart of all is the one<br>that can still love, even while it bleeds, and<br>especially after its been broken into <br>thousands of pieces" ~ Styxx<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388931i/749819.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388931i/749820._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You know, a long time ago, my mentor taught me that there’s only one reason to go to war. To protect the ones you love. But life has taught me that sometimes protecting isn’t about leaving them. It’s about being here when they need you. It doesn’t take courage to die, Acheron. It takes courage to live and to fight.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>Highly Recommended , for a strong heart.</b></span>

<div id="review_375656269" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/375656269" />
    <a title="Steph" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4215697-steph"><img alt="Steph" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346102450p2/4215697.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/375656269?book_show_action=true">Jul 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Steph" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Steph" href="/user/show/4215697-steph">Steph</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781405528214" href="/book/show/18386252-styxx">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=kindle-read">kindle-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer375656269" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6366659358564595589"> I cannot believe that I thought so badly of Styxx before this book. The pain and suffering he faced throughout his life is just unimaginable. <br/> This was an absolutely incredible book, and in ‘Part 2’ it really felt like we were back in the Dark Hunter world. I loved all the crossovers from previous books too.<br/><br/> The reason, well the two reasons I didn’t give this book the full five stars was, One... the first part of the book where we saw Styxx and Acheron’s past again was absolutely brutal and hea</span>
  <span id="freeText6366659358564595589" style="display:none"> I cannot believe that I thought so badly of Styxx before this book. The pain and suffering he faced throughout his life is just unimaginable. <br /> This was an absolutely incredible book, and in ‘Part 2’ it really felt like we were back in the Dark Hunter world. I loved all the crossovers from previous books too.<br /><br /> The reason, well the two reasons I didn’t give this book the full five stars was, One... the first part of the book where we saw Styxx and Acheron’s past again was absolutely brutal and heavy. It felt to me like Sherrilyn Kenyon was trying to make Styxx’s past worse than Acheron’s. It felt a little forced because there was just so much of it.<br /> Some of the rapes scenes just weren’t necessary. By this point, we understand what Apollo and Estes were doing to him we didn’t need to see it quite so many times. And when Styxx was held prisoner for a year? I just felt like it was overkill. <br /><br /> Reason two was the ending <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[About Styxx and Bethany <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Things were going so great, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they could bring her back to life <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and then all of a sudden there’s this huge and complicated story about them in the past life, who he was really supposed to be… it was just too much. The author completely overdid it, again.<br /><br /> But anyway onto the good stuff.<br /><br /> Styxx and Bethany were such a beautiful couple. She definitely saved his life. She was there when he was at one of his lowest points and she gave him someone to trust, someone to love.<br />As much as I hated reading about all the awful things that happened to Styxx, it was great to see how different the same story was, just from Styxx’s point of view.<br /><br /> Ryssa seemed like a completely different person. It was astonishing how one person can be so sweet, caring and kind to Ash. But to Styxx, she was like poison. Every time she came close to him she was spitting insults and making him feel worthless. She was truly despicable to him. I hated the Ryssa we saw in this book.<br /><br /> Apollo… Jesus. If I thought this guy was a monster before, I had no idea. The way he targeted and pursued Styxx was terrifying and disgusting. He made his life a living hell, always being terrified of when Apollo would come for him. Even after his first victory in war, Apollo couldn’t let him be happy. He had to come and destroy him worse than ever before. It was horrifying.<br /><br /> Estes was really the worst thing that ever happened to Styxx. He was the one that started everything off and who separated Styxx and Acheron when they were just children. He drove the wedge between them. <br /><br /> I saw quite a few people saying that they hated Ash while reading this book, and while I understand their reasons I have to say that I could <b>never</b> hate him. Never. I think what people have to remember whilst reading this book is that Styxx and Acheron have been pitted against each other since the very day they were born. Their situation was impossible. They were destined to be destroyed, destined to hate each other. It was heart-breaking. <br /><br /> The very best thing about this book, I think was Styxx and Acheron’s relationship. I loved seeing them more as young boys. Sleeping back to back, sharing toys and being there for each other. They were so sweet together. <br /> Then watching as they were torn apart and reunited thousands of years later… I loved watching their journey.<br /><br /> There wasn’t a huge amount of storyline progression, I have to say. But there was a little bit at the end steering us in the next direction.<br /> There is so much more I could say. So many things happened. It was so good to see Savitar, Nick, Set was brilliant, Appolymi was wonderful (sometimes), Simi is back on form… and so many more.<br /><br /> I am so happy to have gotten a book like this in the series. The last few books have been a bit of a let-down for me. So I have every faith that the next Dark Hunter book will be back to its old standard.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6366659358564595589" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
